I had a slab leak that my HOA was responsible to fix, so we decided to get a couple quotes on the repair.  We were referred to Richco from another plumber that we had used but they weren't available.  When Robert Summers came to check out the leak and quote the job, he looked at the job from a long term perspective, not just a quick fix.  He brought up things the other plumber didn't and we felt we were in good hands so we hired him.  Once the repair started, Robert encountered a problem due to the leak detection company who had marked off the wrong place.  Robert quickly figured out a fix, and although it took more time and money, the job was done well.  Robert and his assistant were always friendly, on time and cleaned up everything each day.  We will definitely be using Richco and requesting Robert Summers again and will also use them for leak detection in the future, rather than hiring a separate company which will hopefully avoid the errors we encountered.</review>

< text>
Our usual place (Joy Luck) was closed! So my Grandpa wanted to go two storefronts down to Gum Wah. It's a big restaurant with lot of seating.
Like Joy Luck restaurant, Gum Wah is what Americans would call a hole in the wall (or to me, normal).
Before I ordered I saw what others were eating. It all looked so good. It was lunchtime and most people ordered lunch special items.
We got chow fun with prawn, rice porridge fish filet, yin yang fried rice, bitter melon lunch special and some typical beef string bean lunch special.
The chow fun was amazing. I loved it! It was so flavorful. It's the saucy style chow fun I like too.
The rice porridge was tasty. It had plenty of fish and 1 whole egg (1000 yr old).
Bitter melon was good for bitter melon.
The yin yang fried rice was the dish I ordered, and it wasn't to par. I was kind of sad. The rice seemed old/dry. The tomato sauce did not have much taste. I think I was unlucky!
I give this place 5 stars because I would get the chow fun again. Another customer had the black bean chow fun... I wanted it...
Would definitely go back!< /text>

<Name>April Diaz<//Name><Time>1448136960417<//Time><rate>4< /rate>< Review>
This is my go to for Chinese porridge. Some porridge places are sheisty with the meat or other fillings in their porridge, but not this place. They give you a good amount of toppings at a really good price. And of course they boil the heck out of that rice, and so you get beautiful cooked down pieces of rice swimming in watery rice broth. Topped off with ginger and cilantro. It's pure class. Classy congee made in a hole in a wall. Dunk in pieces of the youtiao (donuts/cruller) and you're golden! My favorite is the sampan, but all of them are pretty yummy.

Other exceptional items:

Roasted duck
Roasted pork
Shrimp crepe rice roll
Duck won ton and egg noodle soup
Beef stew and egg noodle soup< /Review>

< user_name>
Charles Faulkner<//user_name>
<Gmap_id>0x808fffad7232edc5:0x6395055296371616<//Gmap_id>< Review>
Prior to Quick Quack opening here in Brentwood, I had watched a couple of you tube videos about there carwashes. Not the biggest fan of these type of carwash with the rotating brushes, and so forth but they have come along with the material they use as compared to the older ones.
So Quick Quack finally opens here in Brentwood, and I get a free wash coupon in the mail, so I decide I'm going to give them a try. 1st thing I'II say is this is a good location in my opinion, busy intersection with lots of housing, traffic, and other business's. Set up of this carwash is good. I pull into the vehicle entrance, and am greeted by a QQ employee. Show employee my free wash coupon. She does a walk around of my vehicle, and then proceeds to write on the windshield " 1" with the letters "TR" below that. I assume this is for the employee at the entrance to the wash to key in they type of wash. These type of carwashes basically have 3 basic rules - vehicle in neutral, foot off the break, and hands off the steering wheel. Carwash starts, all seems well until we get to the brush that is suppose to get the hood, windshield, and top of vehicle. Well, I wait and it never came down, so I'm left with a windshield full of bug splatter. Vehicle continues on through the rinse, tire shine, and air dryer. Not happy about the left over bug splatter, I inform one of the QQ employees what happened. I'm not mad or complaining but want them to know what happened. QQ employee offers another wash. I decline, letting him know what happened, thinking there may be mechanical issue. so when you exit wash, you can pull into the vacuum area. QQ offers free vacuums for you to use. So as I'm vacuuming my vehicle, another QQ employee comes over and informs me that the reason the brush did not do the hood, windshield, & top of vehicle was because my vehicle has a top rack, hence "TR" that has 2 braces that go "side to side". He explains that if I remove those 2 braces prior to going thru wash that brush would come down. the employee at the entrance of the wash, uses the code written on your windshield to program what kind of wash your getting. I have used a couple of other places that use this type of wash system, and I have never had an issue with my TR braces. Back to vacuums, they offer 2 types of vacuum nozzles - Crevice type for those hard to reach area's & a wide mouth type for your carpet and mats. Vacuums work well and provide good suction. They also offer an air hose for blowing out your console & dash area, I found the air pressure inadequate. The other issue, I noticed is that there " Tire Shine" did not apply. I checked numerous vehicle & found none of them had the "Tire Shine" applied. So in closing these are my thoughts -  1) overall wash was ok 2) if your top rack has cross bars that go "side to side" you need to remove 3) Tire Shine may or may not apply on that day 4) Vacuum works great 5) Air Hose is okay. So with that being said, it will be up to each individual to decide for themselves if QQ Carwash meets there needs. For me, I'm on the fence about it but love the Duck.<//Review>

<Text>Decent drive through but for the price I thought they would have carwash employees to dry and vacuum your car.

The monthly subscription isnt any better than other places.

< text>
Attention Linda and Drew. We have been residents of Santa Clarita for many years now, but we live closer to the Ralphs in Granary Square. As we were heading back from Los Angeles yesterday, 4/15/2021 - we decided to go to the Stevenson Ranch Ralphs location before heading home. As we walked in we noted that the store was in great order and also the COVID19 guidelines were in place.

I noted that the store was clean and much larger than the location we go to most often.

There was an item that was not on the shelf, so I waived down Drew and asked him if there was any more of this product. He treated me as if I was his only customer and told me he would check. While he was gone, we had changed positions in the store, as we were continuing to shop.

About 10 minutes later, as we had made it to the other side of the store, Drew found us. He had been searching isle by isle. His conscientious demeanor was incredible. He was also attentive and explained that they were out now, however - there were other options as he gave me those.

Drew should be commended on his ability to get the job done as well as his ability to bag groceries the right way, as I was taught when I was his age.

At checkout we were Blessed to have met Linda. She was a breath of fresh air, she was friendly and made us feel as we have been coming to this Ralphs location as often as we visit the Granary location. She also commented on how we were holding hands - that of course made the both of us gush over with happiness that someone would take the time to notice, let alone comment.

Linda and Drew are both Blessings to the Ralphs in Stevenson Ranch. I hope they get commended because we are now going to make this store our primary shopping location.</text>

< Text>
Pickup was great; fast and easy, nice guys. Scheduling was a bit of a miscommunication. While originally told it would be a 2-hour window, which is standard, when I finally set up my date (based on new furniture delivery date), I asked if they could be there early am, like by 8:30. I was told that would be fine, we would be the first stop.
Day of, not so much. I called to relay which parking lot to use at my dad's apartment complex, and was told I had a 10-12 arrival window. This was a problem, because the new furniture was coming within a window that started at 8:45. It was taking away old couch before delivery of new. For my dad's senior apartment, where that's the only seating. Didn't want to leave him for 24 hours or more with no place to sit but his bed, and no room for a second couch!
But Junk Kings was able to divert a crew my way, they arrived before the new couch, and everything worked out. I would use them again, hopefully for a less complex situation...</Text>
